   function getRootDomain(hostname) {
            if (hostname.indexOf('buffalowildwings.com') < 0) {
                return hostname
            }

            var tokens = hostname.split('.')
            if (tokens.length <= 2) {
                return hostname
            }

            var root = tokens.slice(1).join('.')
            return root
        }

        document.domain = getRootDomain(window.location.hostname)
